<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мрачный.html>мра́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mráčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мрачи́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mračítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:омрачить.html>омрачи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">omračítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:омрачать.html>омрача́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to darken, to cloud</li>
<li>to darken, to cloud, to overshadow</li></ol>

<ol><li><i>(underwater)</i> pool, slough

<li>whirlpool</li>
<li>slough
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толкать.html>толка́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:омут.html>о́мут</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tolkátʹ v ómut</i> ― <span class="e-translation">urge on to one's destruction</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:омывать.html>омыва́ть</a> (20417)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:омыть.html>омы́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">omýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:омывать.html>омыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">omyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:омыть.html>омы́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:омыть.html>омы́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doždʹ <b>omýl</b> úlicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the rain <b>washed</b> the streets</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:омыть.html>омы́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">úlicy <b>omýlo</b> doždjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the streets <b>were washed</b> by the rain</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pour over from all sides, to lap <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of water</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to surround with its water <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of the sea or ocean</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мыть.html>мыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:омыть.html>омы́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">omýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:омывать.html>омыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> also  impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:омыть.html>омы́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">doždʹ <b>omýl</b> úlicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the rain <b>washed</b> the streets</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:омыть.html>омы́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дождём</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">úlicy <b>omýlo</b> doždjóm</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the streets <b>were washed</b> by the rain</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***он.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> (4)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">онъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">onŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*onъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">on</span>) (<i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a></b>, <i>neuter</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>оно́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>third-person masculine singular pronoun: he, it.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Whenever a preposition stands immediately before any of the oblique cases of the third-person pronoun (singular or plural) and directly governs it, then an <b>н</b>- must be prefixed to the pronoun: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ot nevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(from him)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">na njóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(on him)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">u nevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(he has)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">k nemú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(to him)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s nim</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(with him)</i>.</li>
<li>The explanation for the <b>н</b>-prothesis is that, originally, some Russian prepositions ended in the letter -<b>н</b>: <b>сън</b> (sŭn, <i>“with”</i>...cf. Greek <b><i class="None mention" lang="ru">σύν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">σύν</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>, Latin <b><span class="Latn" lang="la">cum</span></b>). Eventually, the final <b>н</b> of these prepositions migrated across to the pronoun, so that <b>сън им</b> became modern <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s nim</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and then this was extended to include <i>all</i> prepositions when governing any third-person pronoun.</li>
<li>Note that if the preposition does <b>not</b> directly govern <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e., when <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></b> is a possessive pronoun), then <b>н</b>- is not prefixed: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́та</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">u jevó bráta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(at his brother’s)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">o jevó máteri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(about his mother)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">v jevó kómnate</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(in his room)</i>.</li>
<li>When there is another word separating a preposition and any oblique case of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a></b>, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>н-</a></b> is not added: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">u samovó jevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(with him himself)</i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a></b>
</p><p>Местоимение, <a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:третий.html>тре́тьего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>Фо́рмы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:косвенный.html>ко́свенных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>падеже́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начальный.html>нача́льным</a> <i>н</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ются</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сочетание.html>сочета́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предлог.html>предло́гами</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:мочь.html>мо́жет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ться</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>после</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>сравни́тельной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пени</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>Также</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> предложном <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> творительном <a href = vnd.unilang:падеж.html>падежа́х</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:использоваться.html>испо́льзуется</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="устаревшее">устар.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="диалектное">диал.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="просторечное"><a href = vnd.unilang:простой.html>прост</a>.</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:вариант.html>вариа́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a>: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> ём</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> ём</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> ём</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она</a> (15)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ona</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_3">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oná</span>) (<i>masculine counterpart</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a></b>, <i>neuter counterpart</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>оно́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>she, it <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">third-person feminine singular pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>Да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́т</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Da kak že <b>oná</b>, tak i govorít?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">What is she like? Does she talk?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Её</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>до́ма</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">genitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Jejó</b> net dóma</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><i>She’s not home.</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Ей</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:спаться.html>спи́тся</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Jej</b> ne spítsja.</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><i>She is unable to sleep.</i></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́жу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a></b>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vížu <b>jejó</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I see her.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>не́ю</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рубль.html>рубле́й</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">instrumental</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Za <b>néju</b> pjatʹ rubléj.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She owes five rubles.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a>.</i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">prepositional</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On éto pri <b>nej</b> skazál.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He said it in her presence.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Whenever a preposition stands immediately before any of the oblique cases of the third-person pronoun (singular or plural) and directly governs it, then an <b>н</b>- is prefixed to the pronoun: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ot nejó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">from her</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na nej</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">on her</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u nejó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">she has</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ней</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">k nej</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to her</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>не́ю</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s néju</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with her</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>The explanation for the <b>н</b>-prothesis is that, originally, some Russian prepositions ended in the letter -<b>н</b>: <b>сън</b> (sŭn, <i>“with”</i>...cf. Greek <b><i class="None mention" lang="ru">σύν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">σύν</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>, Latin <b><i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cum</i></b>). Eventually, the final <b>н</b> of these prepositions migrated across to the pronoun, so that <b>вън <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a></b> became modern <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v nejó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and then this was extended to include <i>all</i> prepositions when governing any third-person pronoun.</li>
<li>Note that if the preposition does <b>not</b> directly govern <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jejó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e., when <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a></b> is a possessive pronoun), then the <b>н</b>- is not inserted: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u jejó bráta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">at her brother’s</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o jejó máteri</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">about her mother</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v jejó kómnate</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in her room</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>When there is another word separating a preposition and any oblique case of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она</a></b>, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>н-</a></b> is not added: <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>само́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">u samój jejó</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">with her herself</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a></b>
</p><p>Местоимение, <a href = vnd.unilang:личный.html>ли́чное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:третий.html>тре́тьего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:образовать.html>Образу́ет</a> омоформу <i><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> притяжательным местоимением <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>рода</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:третий.html>тре́тьего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица</a>.

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:вне.html>Вне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тих</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чаев</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребление.html>употребле́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рм</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ея</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>нея́</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <i>оне</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:сегодня.html>сего́дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможно.html>возмо́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:иронический.html>ирони́ческий</a> эрратив.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-он-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>-а</a></b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

***онанизм.html

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:онанизм.html>онани́зм</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">onanízm</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:онанизм.html>онани́зма</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:онанизм.html>онани́змы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:онанизм.html>онани́змов</a></b>)

***онеметь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:онеметь.html>онеметь</a> (10422)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неметь.html>неме́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nemétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:онеметь.html>онеме́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">onemétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неметь.html>неме́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">онемева́ть</b>)
</p>

***они.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они</a> (18)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*onъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">oní</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>they <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">third-person plural pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>An <b>н</b> is prefixed to any third-person pronoun in an oblique case whenever a preposition that directly governs it is immediately in front of it: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>неё</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ot nejó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(from her)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">na njóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(on him)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>них</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">u nix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(they have)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">k nemú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(to him)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>не́ю</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s néju</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(with her)</i>.</li>
<li>This comes from Russian prepositions such as <b>сън</b> (sŭn, "with", cf. Greek <b><i class="None mention" lang="ru">σύν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">σύν</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>, Latin <b><span class="Latn" lang="la">cum</span></b>), that originally ended in -<b>н</b> and governed oblique cases. Since the prepositions and the pronouns occurred together so often, it was easy to lose track of which word the final -<b>н</b> belonged to, and the <b>н</b> was reinterpreted as part of the pronouns (Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">an</i>, in the same way, lost its -n except before vowels, and sometimes gave it to the following word, as in English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">adder</i> from Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">nædre</i>), so that <b>сън <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>и́ми</a></b> became modern <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ни́ми</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s ními</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and this new rule was extended to <i>all</i> prepositions governing any third-person pronoun.</li>
<li>That if the preposition does <b>not</b> directly govern <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jevó, jejó, ix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e., when they are possessive pronouns), then no <b>н</b>- is inserted: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:брат.html>бра́та</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">u jevó bráta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(at his brother’s)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мать.html>ма́тери</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">o jejó máteri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(about her mother)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>их</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комната.html>ко́мнате</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">v ix kómnate</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(in their room)</i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***оно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>оно</a> (289)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>оно́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">onó</span>) (<i>masculine counterpart</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a></b>, <i>feminine counterpart</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>it <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">third-person neuter singular pronoun</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Whenever a preposition stands immediately before any of the oblique cases of the third-person pronoun (singular or plural) and directly governs it, then an <b>н</b>- must be prefixed to the pronoun: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ot nevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(from it)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">na njóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(on it)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">u nevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(it has)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нему́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">k nemú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(to it)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s nim</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(with it)</i>.</li>
<li>The explanation for this <b>н</b>-prothesis is that, originally, some Russian prepositions ended in the letter -<b>н</b>: <b>сън</b> (sŭn, <i>“with”</i>...cf. Greek <b><i class="None mention" lang="ru">σύν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">σύν</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>, Latin <b>cum</b>). Eventually, the final <b>н</b> of these prepositions migrated across to the pronoun, so that <b>сън им</b> became modern <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>ним</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s nim</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and then this was generalized to include <i>all</i> prepositions when governing any third-person pronoun.</li>
<li>Note that if the preposition does <b>not</b> directly govern <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (i.e., when <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is a possessive pronoun), then <b>н</b>- is not prefixed: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́нии</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">v jevó položénii</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(in its position)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ткань.html>тка́ни</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">o jevó tkáni</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(about its fabric)</i>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вес.html>ве́сом</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">s jevó vésom</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(with its weight)</i>.</li>
<li>When there is another word separating a preposition and any oblique case of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>оно</a></b>, the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>н-</a></b> is not added: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">u samovó jevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> <i>(with it itself)</i>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jevó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">svoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:оный.html>о́ный</a> (12342)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*onъ</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оный.html>о́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ónyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">high register</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that, that very, the aforementioned</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that other (as opposed to this)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>о́но</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo vrémja <b>óno</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">of yore; in olden days; once a very long time ago</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>времена́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оный.html>о́ны</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo vremená <b>óny</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">once upon a time; in the old days; once</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дни́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:оный.html>о́ны</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vo dní <b>óny</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">once upon a time; in olden days; once</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> otherworldly, unearthly</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о́</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Местоимение <a href = vnd.unilang:указательный.html>указа́тельное</a>, определительное, адъективное <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. </p>
<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

***опадать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опадать.html>опада́ть</a> (15543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">опад-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opad-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опадать.html>опада́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opadátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опасть.html>опа́сть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of leaves, fruits etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to fall (off)</li>
<li>to subside, to lessen, to diminish, to sink in</li></ol>

***опалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опалить.html>опали́ть</a> (12444)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">palítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опалить.html>опали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опаля́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опа́ливать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to singe (animal, feathers, etc.)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:палить.html>пали́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">palítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опа́ливать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opálivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to sear, to burn, to scorch
<dl><dd><span class="nyms imperfective"><span class="defdate">Imperfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опаля́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opaljátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">опа́ливать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">opálivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опасаться.html>опаса́ться</a> (3185)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опасаться.html>опаса́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opasátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be afraid of, to fear <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to avoid, to beware of, to refrain from <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ genitive or infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опасный.html>опа́сный</a> (1381)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*opasnъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опасный.html>опа́сный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opásnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>dangerous, perilous
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:опасный.html>опа́сная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ция</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сложиться.html>сложи́лась</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Opásnaja</b> situácija složílasʹ.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">A dangerous situation took shape.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">о-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">o-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пасть.html>пасть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pastʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опасть.html>опа́сть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opástʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опадать.html>опада́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of leaves, fruits etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> to fall (off)</li>
<li>to subside, to lessen, to diminish, to sink in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:опасть.html>опа́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лица́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>opál</b> s licá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">his cheeks have sunk in</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***опека.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опека.html>опе́ка</a> (13188)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">орiеkа</i>, a calque of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">prōcūrātor</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">рéčе</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">опі́ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opíka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опека.html>опе́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opéka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опека.html>опе́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опека.html>опе́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опека.html>опе́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>guardianship, wardship, tutelage</li>
<li>trusteeship</li>
<li>guardians, board of guardians</li>
<li>care, surveillance</li></ol>

***опекать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:опекать.html>опека́ть</a> (16475)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:опекать.html>опека́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">opekátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be guardian to, to be trustee to, to have the wardship (of); to be warden to</li>
<li>to patronize; to watch over, to take care of</li></ol>
